Data Envelopment Analysis (DEA)¶

  • Author: Sheng Dai (sheng.dai@aalto.fi)
  • Date : June 5, 2020

Estimating a output oriented VRS model¶

In [1]:
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
In [2]:
# import the package pystoned
from pystoned import DEA
In [3]:
# import data
url = 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/ds2010/pyStoNED-Tutorials/master/Data/firms.csv'
df = pd.read_csv(url, error_bad_lines=False)
df.head(10)

In [4]:
# output
y = df['Energy']

# inputs
x1 = df['OPEX']
x1 = np.asmatrix(x1).T
x2 = df['CAPEX']
x2 = np.asmatrix(x2).T
x = np.concatenate((x1, x2), axis=1)
In [5]:
# define and solve the DEA radial model

orient = "oo"
rts = "vrs"

model = DEA.dea(y, x, orient, rts)

# using local solver (MOSEK API)
from pyomo.opt import SolverFactory
opt = SolverFactory("mosek")
results = opt.solve(model, tee=True)
